MpARA6	Arabidopsis thaliana gene 6		RAB GTPase	genome paper: Mapoly0077s0027.1	Mapoly0077s0027.1; Mp8g00450.1	Bowman, Kohchi, Yamato, et al., Cell 171(2):287-304.e15	28985561	10.1016/j.cell.2017.09.030	Published
MpARF1	AUXIN RESPONSE FACTOR1		Transcription factor, similarity to Arabidopsis activator ARFs.	The M. polymorpha genome encodes three ARFs (MpARF1, MpARF2, and MpARF3). The three MpARFs have a structure common to typical ARFs, containing a B3-like DNA binding domain (DBD) and a protein-protein interaction motif, called domains III and IV (Figs 1A and S2). Between the DBD and domain III, MpARF1 harbors a glutamine-rich region, which is known as a feature of activator ARF members. Phylogenetic analysis showed that MpARF1 belonged to the clade A, which represents activator ARF proteins such as ARF5/MONOPTEROS (MP) of Arabidopsis.	Mapoly0019s0045.1; Mp1g12750.1	Kato et al., PLOS Genet. 11, e1005084 (2015) PMID: 26020919; Flores-Sandval et al., PLOS Genet. 11, e1005207 (2015). PMID: 26020649	PMID: 26020919; PMID: 26020649		Published
MpARF2	AUXIN RESPONSE FACTOR2		Transcription factor, similarity to Arabidopsis repressor ARFs.	MpARF2 resided in clade B, and was shown to function as transcriptional repressor.	Mapoly0011s0167.1; Mp4g11820.1	Kato et al., PLOS Genet. 11, e1005084 (2015) PMID: 26020919; Flores-Sandval et al., PLOS Genet. 11, e1005207 (2015). PMID: 26020649	PMID: 26020919; PMID: 26020649		Published
MpARF3	AUXIN RESPONSE FACTOR3		Transcription factor, similarity to Arabidopsis repressor ARFs.	MpARF3 has a relatively longer DBD, and its domains III and IV show lower similarity to ARFs in the clades A and B. MpARF3 mRNA contains the possible target sequence of microRNA160. These features are common with Arabidopsis ARF10 and ARF16, which possibly function as repressors. Phylogenetic analysis supported the placement of MpARF3 in the clade C including Arabidopsis ARF10, ARF16, and ARF17. MpTUB1	TUB1 (ß-tubulin1)		ß-tubulin	To analyze microtubule function and cell division in Marchantia, the expression of four MpTUBs was compared and TUB1 was found to be most uniformly expressed in Marchantia polymorpha tissues. The live-cell microtubule marker MpTUB1-GFP was generated, which is expressed under the control of the MpEF1a promoter. The observed intimate cooperation of Marchantia polar organizers comprising TUB1 with preprophase bands provides insight into the evolution of division plane alignment control of land plants.
